// ============================================================
// FONCTIONS DE DIAGNOSTIC
// ============================================================

/**
 * Vérifie les pages manquantes
 * 
 * @return void
 */
function checkMissingPages(): void
{
    $requiredPages = [
        'index.php',
        'profil.php',
        'connexion.php',
        'inscription.php',
        'parametres.php',
        'notifications.php',
        'messagerie.php',
        'communautes.php',
        'recherche.php'
    ];
    
    $result = [
        'success' => true,
        'existing' => [],
        'missing' => [],
        'total' => count($requiredPages)
    ];
    
    foreach ($requiredPages as $page) {
        if (file_exists(__DIR__ . '/../' . $page)) {
            $result['existing'][] = $page;
        } else {
            $result['missing'][] = $page;
        }
    }
    
    $result['existing_count'] = count($result['existing']);
    $result['missing_count'] = count($result['missing']);
    
    echo json_encode($result);
}

/**
 * Vérifie les tables manquantes dans la base de données
 * 
 * @return void
 */
function checkMissingTables(): void
{
    global $pdo;
    
    $requiredTables = [
        'utilisateurs',
        'posts',
        'postlike',
        'postcommentaire',
        'ami',
        'message',
        'notifications',
        'communautes',
        'communaute_membres',
        'stories',
        'story_views',
        'ressources',
        'activity_logs',
        'search_history',
        'password_resets'
    ];
    
    try {
        if (!isset($pdo)) {
            echo json_encode(['error' => 'Connexion à la base de données non établie']);
            return;
        }
        
        $existingTables = $pdo->query("SHOW TABLES")->fetchAll(PDO::FETCH_COLUMN);
        
        $result = [
            'success' => true,
            'existing' => [],
            'missing' => [],
            'total' => count($requiredTables)
        ];
        
        foreach ($requiredTables as $table) {
            if (in_array($table, $existingTables)) {
                $result['existing'][] = $table;
            } else {
                $result['missing'][] = $table;
            }
        }
        
        $result['existing_count'] = count($result['existing']);
        $result['missing_count'] = count($result['missing']);
        
        echo json_encode($result);
        
    } catch (PDOException $e) {
        echo json_encode([
            'error' => 'Erreur de connexion à la base de données',
            'message' => $e->getMessage()
        ]);
    }
}
?>

<?php
require_once '../config.php';

if (!is_logged_in()) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Non authentifié'], 401);
}

header('Content-Type: application/json');

$method = $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'];
$input = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true) ?? $_POST;
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Vérifier CSRF pour les actions destructrices
if (in_array($method, ['POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE']) && !verify_csrf_token($input['csrf_token'] ?? '')) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Token CSRF invalide'], 403);
}

switch ($method) {
    case 'GET':
        $action = $_GET['action'] ?? 'list';
        
        switch ($action) {
            case 'list':
                // Liste des amis - CORRIGÉ
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT u.id, u.surnom, u.prenom, u.nom, u.avatar, u.status,
                           a.date_acceptation as friends_since
                    FROM ami a
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON (a.id = ? AND a.idami = u.id) OR (a.idami = ? AND a.id = u.id)
                    WHERE a.accepterami = 1
                    ORDER BY a.date_acceptation DESC
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $userId]);
                $friends = $stmt->fetchAll();
                
                json_response(['success' => true, 'friends' => $friends, 'count' => count($friends)]);
                break;

            case 'requests_received':
                // Demandes reçues en attente - CORRIGÉ
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT u.id, u.surnom, u.prenom, u.nom, u.avatar, a.date_demande
                    FROM ami a
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON a.id = u.id
                    WHERE a.idami = ? AND a.demandeami = 1 AND a.accepterami = 0
                    ORDER BY a.date_demande DESC
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId]);
                $requests = $stmt->fetchAll();
                
                json_response(['success' => true, 'requests' => $requests, 'count' => count($requests)]);
                break;

            case 'requests_sent':
                // Demandes envoyées en attente - CORRIGÉ
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT u.id, u.surnom, u.prenom, u.nom, u.avatar, a.date_demande
                    FROM ami a
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON a.idami = u.id
                    WHERE a.id = ? AND a.demandeami = 1 AND a.accepterami = 0
                    ORDER BY a.date_demande DESC
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId]);
                $requests = $stmt->fetchAll();
                
                json_response(['success' => true, 'requests_sent' => $requests, 'count' => count($requests)]);
                break;

            case 'status':
                $targetId = intval($_GET['user_id'] ?? 0);
                if (!$targetId) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'user_id requis'], 400);
                }

                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT demandeami, accepterami,
                           CASE 
                               WHEN id = ? THEN 'sent'
                               WHEN idami = ? THEN 'received'
                           END as direction
                    FROM ami 
                    WHERE (id = ? AND idami = ?) OR (id = ? AND idami = ?)
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $userId, $userId, $targetId, $targetId, $userId]);
                $relation = $stmt->fetch();

                $status = 'none';
                if ($relation) {
                    if ($relation['accepterami']) {
                        $status = 'friends';
                    } elseif ($relation['demandeami']) {
                        $status = $relation['direction'] === 'sent' ? 'pending_sent' : 'pending_received';
                    }
                }

                json_response(['success' => true, 'status' => $status, 'user_id' => $targetId]);
                break;

            case 'suggestions':
                // Suggestions d'amis - CORRIGÉ
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT u.id, u.surnom, u.prenom, u.nom, u.avatar, u.universite
                    FROM utilisateurs u
                    WHERE u.id != ? 
                    AND u.id NOT IN (
                        SELECT CASE WHEN id = ? THEN idami ELSE id END
                        FROM ami WHERE (id = ? OR idami = ?) AND (accepterami = 1 OR demandeami = 1)
                    )
                    AND u.is_active = 1
                    ORDER BY RAND()
                    LIMIT 10
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $userId, $userId, $userId]);
                $suggestions = $stmt->fetchAll();
                
                json_response(['success' => true, 'suggestions' => $suggestions]);
                break;

            default:
                json_response(['error' => 'Action inconnue'], 400);
        }
        break;

    case 'POST':
        $action = $input['action'] ?? '';
        
        switch ($action) {
            case 'send_request':
                $targetId = intval($input['user_id'] ?? 0);
                
                if ($targetId === $userId) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Vous ne pouvez pas vous ajouter vous-même'], 400);
                }
                
                if ($targetId <= 0) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'ID utilisateur invalide'], 400);
                }

                // Vérifier si l'utilisateur existe
                $checkStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT id FROM utilisateurs WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1");
                $checkStmt->execute([$targetId]);
                if (!$checkStmt->fetch()) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Utilisateur non trouvé'], 404);
                }

                // Vérifier si une relation existe déjà
                $checkRelation = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT * FROM ami 
                    WHERE (id = ? AND idami = ?) OR (id = ? AND idami = ?)
                ");
                $checkRelation->execute([$userId, $targetId, $targetId, $userId]);
                if ($checkRelation->fetch()) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Une demande existe déjà'], 409);
                }

                // Créer la demande
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO ami (id, idami, demandeami, date_demande) VALUES (?, ?, 1, NOW())");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $targetId]);
                $friendshipId = $pdo->lastInsertId();

                // Créer notification pour le destinataire
                $notifStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    INSERT INTO notifications (user_id, type, title, actor_id, link, created_at, is_read) 
                    VALUES (?, 'friend_request', 'Nouvelle demande d\\'ami', ?, 'profil.php?id={$userId}', NOW(), 0)
                ");
                $notifStmt->execute([$targetId, $userId]);

                log_activity($pdo, $userId, 'friend_request_sent', ['target_id' => $targetId]);
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true, 
                    'message' => 'Demande envoyée',
                    'friendship_id' => $friendshipId
                ]);
                break;

            case 'accept_request':
                $targetId = intval($input['user_id'] ?? 0);
                
                // Vérifier que la demande existe et est destinée à l'utilisateur courant
                $checkStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT * FROM ami 
                    WHERE id = ? AND idami = ? AND demandeami = 1 AND accepterami = 0
                ");
                $checkStmt->execute([$targetId, $userId]);
                $request = $checkStmt->fetch();
                
                if (!$request) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Demande non trouvée'], 404);
                }

                // Accepter la demande
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    UPDATE ami SET accepterami = 1, date_acceptation = NOW() 
                    WHERE id = ? AND idami = ?
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$targetId, $userId]);

                // Notifier l'expéditeur
                $notifStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    INSERT INTO notifications (user_id, type, title, actor_id, link, created_at, is_read) 
                    VALUES (?, 'friend_accept', 'A accepté votre demande d\\'ami', ?, 'profil.php?id={$userId}', NOW(), 0)
                ");
                $notifStmt->execute([$targetId, $userId]);

                log_activity($pdo, $userId, 'friend_request_accepted', ['friend_id' => $targetId]);
                
                json_response(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Demande acceptée']);
                break;

            case 'reject_request':
                $targetId = intval($input['user_id'] ?? 0);
                
                // Supprimer la demande
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    DELETE FROM ami 
                    WHERE id = ? AND idami = ? AND demandeami = 1 AND accepterami = 0
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$targetId, $userId]);
                
                if ($stmt->rowCount() === 0) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Demande non trouvée'], 404);
                }

                log_activity($pdo, $userId, 'friend_request_rejected', ['user_id' => $targetId]);
                json_response(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Demande rejetée']);
                break;

            case 'cancel_request':
                $targetId = intval($input['user_id'] ?? 0);
                
                // Annuler une demande envoyée
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    DELETE FROM ami 
                    WHERE id = ? AND idami = ? AND demandeami = 1 AND accepterami = 0
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $targetId]);
                
                if ($stmt->rowCount() === 0) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Demande non trouvée'], 404);
                }

                log_activity($pdo, $userId, 'friend_request_cancelled', ['user_id' => $targetId]);
                json_response(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Demande annulée']);
                break;

            case 'remove_friend':
                $targetId = intval($input['user_id'] ?? 0);
                
                // Supprimer l'amitié dans les deux sens
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    DELETE FROM ami 
                    WHERE (id = ? AND idami = ?) OR (id = ? AND idami = ?)
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $targetId, $targetId, $userId]);
                
                if ($stmt->rowCount() === 0) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Amitié non trouvée'], 404);
                }

                log_activity($pdo, $userId, 'friend_removed', ['user_id' => $targetId]);
                json_response(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Amitié supprimée']);
                break;

            default:
                json_response(['error' => 'Action non reconnue'], 400);
        }
        break;

    default:
        json_response(['error' => 'Méthode non supportée'], 405);
}
?>


<?php
require_once '../config.php';

// Vérification authentification API
if (!is_logged_in()) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Non authentifié'], 401);
}

header('Content-Type: application/json');

$method = $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'];
$input = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true) ?? $_POST;
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Vérifier CSRF pour les actions de modification
if (in_array($method, ['POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE']) && !verify_csrf_token($input['csrf_token'] ?? '')) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Token CSRF invalide'], 403);
}

switch ($method) {
    case 'GET':
        // Récupérer les notifications
        $limit = min(intval($_GET['limit'] ?? 20), 50);
        $offset = intval($_GET['offset'] ?? 0);
        $unreadOnly = isset($_GET['unread']) && $_GET['unread'] === '1';
        
        $sql = "SELECT n.*, u.surnom as actor_name, u.avatar as actor_avatar 
                FROM notifications n 
                LEFT JOIN utilisateurs u ON n.actor_id = u.id 
                WHERE n.user_id = ?";
        
        if ($unreadOnly) {
            $sql .= " AND n.is_read = 0";
        }
        
        $sql .= " ORDER BY n.created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?";
        
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare($sql);
        $stmt->execute([$userId, $limit, $offset]);
        $notifications = $stmt->fetchAll();
        
        // Compter les non-lues
        $countStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM notifications WHERE user_id = ? AND is_read = 0");
        $countStmt->execute([$userId]);
        $unreadCount = $countStmt->fetchColumn();
        
        json_response([
            'success' => true,
            'notifications' => $notifications,
            'unread_count' => $unreadCount,
            'has_more' => count($notifications) === $limit
        ]);
        break;

    case 'POST':
        $action = $input['action'] ?? '';
        
        switch ($action) {
            case 'create':
                // Créer une notification (utilisé par d'autres parties du système)
                if ($_SESSION['role'] !== 'admin') {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Permission refusée'], 403);
                }
                
                $targetUserId = intval($input['user_id'] ?? 0);
                $type = $input['type'] ?? '';
                $title = trim($input['title'] ?? '');
                $message = trim($input['message'] ?? '');
                $link = trim($input['link'] ?? '');
                $actorId = isset($input['actor_id']) ? intval($input['actor_id']) : null;
                
                $validTypes = ['like', 'comment', 'friend_request', 'friend_accept', 'mention', 'post', 'system'];
                if (!in_array($type, $validTypes)) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Type invalide'], 400);
                }
                
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO notifications 
                    (user_id, type, title, message, link, actor_id) 
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)");
                $stmt->execute([$targetUserId, $type, $title, $message, $link, $actorId]);
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true,
                    'id' => $pdo->lastInsertId()
                ]);
                break;

            case 'mark_read':
                // Marquer une ou plusieurs notifications comme lues
                $notifId = isset($input['id']) ? intval($input['id']) : null;
                
                if ($notifId) {
                    // Marquer une spécifique
                    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE notifications SET is_read = 1 
                        WHERE id = ? AND user_id = ?");
                    $stmt->execute([$notifId, $userId]);
                } else {
                    // Marquer toutes comme lues
                    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE notifications SET is_read = 1 WHERE user_id = ?");
                    $stmt->execute([$userId]);
                }
                
                // Récupérer le nouveau compte
                $countStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM notifications WHERE user_id = ? AND is_read = 0");
                $countStmt->execute([$userId]);
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true,
                    'marked' => $stmt->rowCount(),
                    'unread_count' => $countStmt->fetchColumn()
                ]);
                break;

            case 'mark_unread':
                $notifId = intval($input['id'] ?? 0);
                
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE notifications SET is_read = 0 
                    WHERE id = ? AND user_id = ?");
                $stmt->execute([$notifId, $userId]);
                
                json_response(['success' => true]);
                break;

            default:
                json_response(['error' => 'Action non reconnue'], 400);
        }
        break;

    case 'DELETE':
        $notifId = intval($input['id'] ?? $_GET['id'] ?? 0);
        
        if (!$notifId) {
            json_response(['error' => 'ID requis'], 400);
        }
        
        // Vérifier CSRF pour la suppression (déjà fait en haut)
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM notifications WHERE id = ? AND user_id = ?");
        $stmt->execute([$notifId, $userId]);
        
        if ($stmt->rowCount() === 0) {
            json_response(['error' => 'Notification non trouvée'], 404);
        }
        
        json_response(['success' => true, 'deleted' => $notifId]);
        break;

    default:
        json_response(['error' => 'Méthode non supportée'], 405);
}
?>


<?php
require_once '../config.php';

if (!is_logged_in()) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Non authentifié'], 401);
}

header('Content-Type: application/json');

$method = $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'];
$input = json_decode(file_get_contents('php://input'), true) ?? $_POST;
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Vérifier CSRF pour les actions de modification
if (in_array($method, ['POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE']) && !verify_csrf_token($input['csrf_token'] ?? '')) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Token CSRF invalide'], 403);
}

switch ($method) {
    case 'GET':
        $action = $_GET['action'] ?? 'feed';
        
        switch ($action) {
            case 'feed':
                // Fil d'actualité personnalisé
                $limit = min(intval($_GET['limit'] ?? 10), 50);
                $offset = intval($_GET['offset'] ?? 0);
                
                // Posts des amis + posts publics + posts de l'utilisateur
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT p.*, u.surnom, u.avatar, u.prenom, u.nom,
                           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM postlike WHERE idpost = p.idpost) as likes_count,
                           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM postcommentaire WHERE idpost = p.idpost) as comments_count,
                           (SELECT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM postlike WHERE idpost = p.idpost AND id = ?)) as user_liked
                    FROM posts p
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON p.id_utilisateur = u.id
                    WHERE p.id_utilisateur = ? 
                       OR p.id_utilisateur IN (
                           SELECT CASE WHEN id = ? THEN idami ELSE id END 
                           FROM ami WHERE (id = ? OR idami = ?) AND accepterami = 1
                       )
                    ORDER BY p.date_publication DESC
                    LIMIT ? OFFSET ?
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $userId, $userId, $userId, $userId, $limit, $offset]);
                $posts = $stmt->fetchAll();
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true, 
                    'posts' => $posts,
                    'has_more' => count($posts) === $limit
                ]);
                break;

            case 'user':
                // Posts d'un utilisateur spécifique
                $targetId = intval($_GET['user_id'] ?? $userId);
                $limit = min(intval($_GET['limit'] ?? 20), 50);
                $offset = intval($_GET['offset'] ?? 0);
                
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT p.*, u.surnom, u.avatar,
                           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM postlike WHERE idpost = p.idpost) as likes_count,
                           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM postcommentaire WHERE idpost = p.idpost) as comments_count,
                           (SELECT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM postlike WHERE idpost = p.idpost AND id = ?)) as user_liked
                    FROM posts p
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON p.id_utilisateur = u.id
                    WHERE p.id_utilisateur = ?
                    ORDER BY p.date_publication DESC
                    LIMIT ? OFFSET ?
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $targetId, $limit, $offset]);
                $posts = $stmt->fetchAll();
                
                json_response(['success' => true, 'posts' => $posts]);
                break;

            case 'single':
                // Un post spécifique avec commentaires
                $postId = intval($_GET['id'] ?? 0);
                
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT p.*, u.surnom, u.avatar, u.prenom, u.nom,
                           (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM postlike WHERE idpost = p.idpost) as likes_count,
                           (SELECT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM postlike WHERE idpost = p.idpost AND id = ?)) as user_liked
                    FROM posts p
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON p.id_utilisateur = u.id
                    WHERE p.idpost = ?
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $postId]);
                $post = $stmt->fetch();
                
                if (!$post) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Post non trouvé'], 404);
                }

                // Commentaires
                $commentsStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT c.*, u.surnom, u.avatar
                    FROM postcommentaire c
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON c.id = u.id
                    WHERE c.idpost = ?
                    ORDER BY c.datecommentaire DESC
                    LIMIT 50
                ");
                $commentsStmt->execute([$postId]);
                $comments = $commentsStmt->fetchAll();
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true, 
                    'post' => $post,
                    'comments' => $comments
                ]);
                break;

            default:
                json_response(['error' => 'Action inconnue'], 400);
        }
        break;

    case 'POST':
        $action = $input['action'] ?? 'create';
        
        switch ($action) {
            case 'create':
                $content = trim($input['content'] ?? '');
                $privacy = in_array($input['privacy'] ?? 'public', ['public', 'friends', 'private']) 
                    ? $input['privacy'] 
                    : 'public';
                
                if (empty($content) && empty($_FILES['image'])) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Contenu requis'], 400);
                }

                $imagePath = null;
                
                // Gestion de l'upload d'image
                if (isset($_FILES['image']) && $_FILES['image']['error'] === UPLOAD_ERR_OK) {
                    $upload = handle_file_upload($_FILES['image'], POSTS_DIR, 
                        ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/gif', 'image/webp'], 10*1024*1024);
                    
                    if (!$upload['success']) {
                        json_response(['error' => $upload['error']], 400);
                    }
                    $imagePath = $upload['filename'];
                }

                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    INSERT INTO posts (id_utilisateur, contenu, image_post, privacy, date_publication) 
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, NOW())
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $content, $imagePath, $privacy]);
                $postId = $pdo->lastInsertId();

                // Créer des notifications pour les amis (si public ou amis)
                if ($privacy !== 'private') {
                    $friendsStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                        SELECT CASE WHEN id = ? THEN idami ELSE id END as friend_id
                        FROM ami WHERE (id = ? OR idami = ?) AND accepterami = 1
                    ");
                    $friendsStmt->execute([$userId, $userId, $userId]);
                    $friends = $friendsStmt->fetchAll();
                    
                    $notifStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                        INSERT INTO notifications (user_id, type, title, actor_id, link) 
                        VALUES (?, 'post', 'Nouvelle publication', ?, 'index.php?post={$postId}')
                    ");
                    foreach ($friends as $friend) {
                        $notifStmt->execute([$friend['friend_id'], $userId]);
                    }
                }

                log_activity($pdo, $userId, 'post_created', ['post_id' => $postId]);
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true,
                    'post_id' => $postId,
                    'message' => 'Publication créée'
                ]);
                break;

            case 'like':
                $postId = intval($input['post_id'] ?? 0);
                
                // Vérifier si déjà liké
                $checkStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT idlike FROM postlike WHERE idpost = ? AND id = ?");
                $checkStmt->execute([$postId, $userId]);
                
                if ($checkStmt->fetch()) {
                    // Unlike
                    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM postlike WHERE idpost = ? AND id = ?");
                    $stmt->execute([$postId, $userId]);
                    $liked = false;
                } else {
                    // Like
                    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("INSERT INTO postlike (idpost, id) VALUES (?, ?)");
                    $stmt->execute([$postId, $userId]);
                    $liked = true;
                    
                    // Notifier l'auteur du post (sauf si c'est soi-même)
                    $authorStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT id_utilisateur FROM posts WHERE idpost = ?");
                    $authorStmt->execute([$postId]);
                    $authorId = $authorStmt->fetchColumn();
                    
                    if ($authorId && $authorId != $userId) {
                        $notifStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                            INSERT INTO notifications (user_id, type, title, actor_id, link) 
                            VALUES (?, 'like', 'A aimé votre publication', ?, 'index.php?post={$postId}')
                        ");
                        $notifStmt->execute([$authorId, $userId]);
                    }
                }

                // Compter les likes totaux
                $countStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM postlike WHERE idpost = ?");
                $countStmt->execute([$postId]);
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true,
                    'liked' => $liked,
                    'likes_count' => $countStmt->fetchColumn()
                ]);
                break;

            case 'comment':
                $postId = intval($input['post_id'] ?? 0);
                $content = trim($input['content'] ?? '');
                
                if (empty($content)) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Commentaire vide'], 400);
                }

                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    INSERT INTO postcommentaire (idpost, id, textecommentaire, datecommentaire) 
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, NOW())
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$postId, $userId, $content]);
                $commentId = $pdo->lastInsertId();

                // Notifier l'auteur du post
                $authorStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT id_utilisateur FROM posts WHERE idpost = ?");
                $authorStmt->execute([$postId]);
                $authorId = $authorStmt->fetchColumn();
                
                if ($authorId && $authorId != $userId) {
                    $notifStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                        INSERT INTO notifications (user_id, type, title, actor_id, link) 
                        VALUES (?, 'comment', 'A commenté votre publication', ?, 'index.php?post={$postId}')
                    ");
                    $notifStmt->execute([$authorId, $userId]);
                }

                // Retourner le commentaire créé avec infos utilisateur
                $commentStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    SELECT c.*, u.surnom, u.avatar 
                    FROM postcommentaire c
                    JOIN utilisateurs u ON c.id = u.id
                    WHERE c.idcommentaire = ?
                ");
                $commentStmt->execute([$commentId]);
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true,
                    'comment' => $commentStmt->fetch()
                ]);
                break;

            case 'share':
                $postId = intval($input['post_id'] ?? 0);
                $comment = trim($input['comment'] ?? '');
                
                // Récupérer le post original
                $originalStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM posts WHERE idpost = ?");
                $originalStmt->execute([$postId]);
                $original = $originalStmt->fetch();
                
                if (!$original) {
                    json_response(['error' => 'Post non trouvé'], 404);
                }

                // Créer un nouveau post avec référence
                $content = $comment ? $comment . "\n\n[shared]" . $original['contenu'] : "[shared]" . $original['contenu'];
                
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    INSERT INTO posts (id_utilisateur, contenu, image_post, shared_from, date_publication) 
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, NOW())
                ");
                $stmt->execute([$userId, $content, $original['image_post'], $postId]);
                
                json_response([
                    'success' => true,
                    'post_id' => $pdo->lastInsertId(),
                    'message' => 'Partagé avec succès'
                ]);
                break;

            default:
                json_response(['error' => 'Action non reconnue'], 400);
        }
        break;

    case 'PUT':
        // Modifier un post
        $postId = intval($input['post_id'] ?? 0);
        $content = trim($input['content'] ?? '');
        
        // Vérifier propriétaire
        $checkStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT id_utilisateur FROM posts WHERE idpost = ?");
        $checkStmt->execute([$postId]);
        $ownerId = $checkStmt->fetchColumn();
        
        if ($ownerId != $userId && $_SESSION['role'] !== 'admin') {
            json_response(['error' => 'Permission refusée'], 403);
        }

        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE posts SET contenu = ?, edited_at = NOW() WHERE idpost = ?");
        $stmt->execute([$content, $postId]);
        
        json_response(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Post modifié']);
        break;

    case 'DELETE':
        $postId = intval($input['post_id'] ?? $_GET['post_id'] ?? 0);
        
        // Vérifier propriétaire
        $checkStmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT id_utilisateur, image_post FROM posts WHERE idpost = ?");
        $checkStmt->execute([$postId]);
        $post = $checkStmt->fetch();
        
        if (!$post) {
            json_response(['error' => 'Post non trouvé'], 404);
        }
        
        if ($post['id_utilisateur'] != $userId && $_SESSION['role'] !== 'admin') {
            json_response(['error' => 'Permission refusée'], 403);
        }

        // Supprimer l'image associée si existe
        if ($post['image_post'] && file_exists(POSTS_DIR . $post['image_post'])) {
            unlink(POSTS_DIR . $post['image_post']);
        }

        // Supprimer les likes et commentaires associés (cascade en DB normalement)
        $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM postlike WHERE idpost = ?")->execute([$postId]);
        $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM postcommentaire WHERE idpost = ?")->execute([$postId]);
        
        // Supprimer le post
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM posts WHERE idpost = ?");
        $stmt->execute([$postId]);

        log_activity($pdo, $userId, 'post_deleted', ['post_id' => $postId]);
        
        json_response(['success' => true, 'message' => 'Post supprimé']);
        break;

    default:
        json_response(['error' => 'Méthode non supportée'], 405);
}

<?php
require_once '../config.php';

if (!is_logged_in()) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Non authentifié'], 401);
}

header('Content-Type: application/json');

$query = trim($_GET['q'] ?? '');
$type = $_GET['type'] ?? 'all'; // all, users, posts, communities
$limit = min(intval($_GET['limit'] ?? 20), 50);
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

if (empty($query) || strlen($query) < 2) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Requête trop courte (min 2 caractères)'], 400);
}

$results = [];
$searchTerm = "%$query%";

// Recherche d'utilisateurs
if (in_array($type, ['all', 'users'])) {
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
        SELECT u.id, u.surnom, u.prenom, u.nom, u.avatar, u.universite, u.profession,
               CASE 
                   WHEN a.accepterami = 1 THEN 'friends'
                   WHEN a.demandeami = 1 AND a.id = ? THEN 'pending_sent'
                   WHEN a.demandeami = 1 AND a.idami = ? THEN 'pending_received'
                   ELSE 'none'
               END as friendship_status
        FROM utilisateurs u
        LEFT JOIN ami a ON (a.id = u.id AND a.idami = ?) OR (a.id = ? AND a.idami = u.id)
        WHERE u.id != ? 
        AND u.is_active = 1
        AND (u.surnom LIKE ? OR u.prenom LIKE ? OR u.nom LIKE ? OR u.email LIKE ?)
        ORDER BY 
            CASE WHEN u.surnom LIKE ? THEN 0 ELSE 1 END,
            u.surnom
        LIMIT ?
    ");
    $exactTerm = "$query%";
    $stmt->execute([
        $userId, $userId, $userId, $userId, $userId,
        $searchTerm, $searchTerm, $searchTerm, $searchTerm,
        $exactTerm, $limit
    ]);
    $results['users'] = $stmt->fetchAll();
}

// Recherche de posts
if (in_array($type, ['all', 'posts'])) {
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
        SELECT p.idpost, p.contenu, p.image_post, p.date_publication,
               u.id as user_id, u.surnom, u.avatar,
               (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM postlike WHERE idpost = p.idpost) as likes_count
        FROM posts p
        JOIN utilisateurs u ON p.id_utilisateur = u.id
        WHERE p.contenu LIKE ? 
        AND (p.id_utilisateur = ? OR p.id_utilisateur IN (
            SELECT CASE WHEN id = ? THEN idami ELSE id END 
            FROM ami WHERE (id = ? OR idami = ?) AND accepterami = 1
        ))
        ORDER BY p.date_publication DESC
        LIMIT ?
    ");
    $stmt->execute([$searchTerm, $userId, $userId, $userId, $userId, $limit]);
    $results['posts'] = $stmt->fetchAll();
}

// Recherche de communautés
if (in_array($type, ['all', 'communities'])) {
    try {
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
            SELECT c.id_communaute, c.nom, c.description, c.categorie, c.image_couverture,
                   (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM communaute_membres WHERE id_communaute = c.id_communaute) as members_count,
                   EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM communaute_membres WHERE id_communaute = c.id_communaute AND id_utilisateur = ?) as is_member
            FROM communautes c
            WHERE c.nom LIKE ? OR c.description LIKE ?
            ORDER BY members_count DESC
            LIMIT ?
        ");
        $stmt->execute([$userId, $searchTerm, $searchTerm, $limit]);
        $results['communities'] = $stmt->fetchAll();
    } catch (PDOException $e) {
        $results['communities'] = [];
    }
}

// Historique de recherche (optionnel - stocker les recherches)
if ($type === 'all') {
    try {
        // Vérifier si la table existe avant d'insérer
        $tableCheck = $pdo->query("SHOW TABLES LIKE 'search_history'");
        if ($tableCheck->rowCount() > 0) {
            $historyStmt = $pdo->prepare("
                INSERT INTO search_history (user_id, query, searched_at) 
                VALUES (?, ?, NOW())
                ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE searched_at = NOW()
            ");
            $historyStmt->execute([$userId, substr($query, 0, 255)]);
        }
    } catch (PDOException $e) {
        // Ignorer silencieusement
    }
}

// Suggestions si peu de résultats
$suggestions = [];
if (count($results['users'] ?? []) < 5) {
    $suggStmt = $pdo->prepare("
        SELECT u.id, u.surnom, u.prenom, u.nom, u.avatar, u.universite
        FROM utilisateurs u
        WHERE u.id != ? AND u.is_active = 1
        AND u.id NOT IN (
            SELECT CASE WHEN id = ? THEN idami ELSE id END
            FROM ami WHERE (id = ? OR idami = ?) AND accepterami = 1
        )
        AND u.id NOT IN (
            SELECT CASE WHEN id = ? THEN idami ELSE id END
            FROM ami WHERE (id = ? OR idami = ?) AND demandeami = 1
        )
        ORDER BY RAND()
        LIMIT 5
    ");
    $suggStmt->execute([$userId, $userId, $userId, $userId, $userId, $userId, $userId]);
    $suggestions = $suggStmt->fetchAll();
}

json_response([
    'success' => true,
    'query' => $query,
    'results' => $results,
    'suggestions' => $suggestions,
    'total_count' => array_sum(array_map('count', $results))
]);
?>



<?php
require_once '../config.php';

if (!is_logged_in()) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Non authentifié'], 401);
}

// Vérifier CSRF
if (!verify_csrf_token($_POST['csrf_token'] ?? $_GET['csrf_token'] ?? '')) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Token CSRF invalide'], 403);
}

header('Content-Type: application/json');

$type = $_GET['type'] ?? 'image';
$context = $_GET['context'] ?? 'general'; // avatar, post, cover, message

// Configuration par type
$configs = [
    'avatar' => [
        'dir' => AVATAR_DIR,
        'max_size' => 2 * 1024 * 1024, // 2MB
        'types' => ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/gif', 'image/webp'],
        'exts' => ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'webp'],
        'resize' => [400, 400]
    ],
    'post' => [
        'dir' => POSTS_DIR,
        'max_size' => 10 * 1024 * 1024, // 10MB
        'types' => ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/gif', 'image/webp', 'video/mp4', 'video/webm'],
        'exts' => ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'webp', 'mp4', 'webm'],
        'resize' => [1920, 1080]
    ],
    'cover' => [
        'dir' => UPLOAD_DIR . 'covers/',
        'max_size' => 5 * 1024 * 1024, // 5MB
        'types' => ['image/jpeg', 'image/png'],
        'exts' => ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png'],
        'resize' => [1500, 500]
    ],
    'message' => [
        'dir' => UPLOAD_DIR . 'messages/',
        'max_size' => 50 * 1024 * 1024, // 50MB
        'types' => ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/gif', 'application/pdf', 'application/msword', 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document', 'video/mp4'],
        'exts' => ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'pdf', 'doc', 'docx', 'mp4'],
        'resize' => false
    ]
];

$config = $configs[$context] ?? $configs['post'];

// Vérifier fichier
if (!isset($_FILES['file']) || $_FILES['file']['error'] !== UPLOAD_ERR_OK) {
    $errors = [
        UPLOAD_ERR_INI_SIZE => 'Fichier trop grand (serveur)',
        UPLOAD_ERR_FORM_SIZE => 'Fichier trop grand (formulaire)',
        UPLOAD_ERR_PARTIAL => 'Upload partiel',
        UPLOAD_ERR_NO_FILE => 'Aucun fichier envoyé',
        UPLOAD_ERR_NO_TMP_DIR => 'Dossier temporaire manquant',
        UPLOAD_ERR_CANT_WRITE => 'Erreur écriture disque',
        UPLOAD_ERR_EXTENSION => 'Extension PHP bloquée'
    ];
    $errorCode = $_FILES['file']['error'] ?? UPLOAD_ERR_NO_FILE;
    json_response(['error' => $errors[$errorCode] ?? 'Erreur upload'], 400);
}

$file = $_FILES['file'];

// Vérifier taille
if ($file['size'] > $config['max_size']) {
    json_response([
        'error' => 'Fichier trop volumineux', 
        'max_size' => $config['max_size'],
        'size' => $file['size']
    ], 400);
}

// Vérifier type MIME réel
$finfo = finfo_open(FILEINFO_MIME_TYPE);
$mime = finfo_file($finfo, $file['tmp_name']);
finfo_close($finfo);

$allowed = false;
foreach ($config['types'] as $type) {
    if ($mime === $type) {
        $allowed = true;
        break;
    }
}

if (!$allowed) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Type de fichier non autorisé: ' . $mime], 400);
}

// Vérifier extension
$ext = strtolower(pathinfo($file['name'], PATHINFO_EXTENSION));
if (!in_array($ext, $config['exts'])) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Extension non autorisée'], 400);
}

// Créer dossier si nécessaire
if (!is_dir($config['dir'])) {
    mkdir($config['dir'], 0755, true);
}

// Générer nom unique
$filename = uniqid() . '_' . bin2hex(random_bytes(4)) . '.' . $ext;
$destination = $config['dir'] . $filename;

// Déplacer fichier
if (!move_uploaded_file($file['tmp_name'], $destination)) {
    json_response(['error' => 'Erreur lors du déplacement'], 500);
}

// Redimensionner si image et config demandée
if ($config['resize'] && in_array($mime, ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/gif', 'image/webp'])) {
    resize_image($destination, $config['resize'][0], $config['resize'][1]);
}

// Log
log_activity($pdo, $_SESSION['user_id'], 'file_uploaded', [
    'context' => $context,
    'filename' => $filename,
    'size' => $file['size']
]);

// Construire l'URL correcte
$baseUrl = rtrim(SITE_URL, '/') . '/';
$relativePath = str_replace($_SERVER['DOCUMENT_ROOT'] . '/', '', $destination);
$url = $baseUrl . $relativePath;

json_response([
    'success' => true,
    'filename' => $filename,
    'url' => $url,
    'size' => $file['size'],
    'mime' => $mime
]);

// Fonction de redimensionnement
function resize_image($path, $max_width, $max_height) {
    if (!extension_loaded('gd')) return false;
    
    list($width, $height) = getimagesize($path);
    
    if ($width <= $max_width && $height <= $max_height) return true;
    
    $ratio = min($max_width / $width, $max_height / $height);
    $new_width = round($width * $ratio);
    $new_height = round($height * $ratio);
    
    $src = imagecreatefromstring(file_get_contents($path));
    $dst = imagecreatetruecolor($new_width, $new_height);
    
    imagecopyresampled($dst, $src, 0, 0, 0, 0, $new_width, $new_height, $width, $height);
    
    $ext = strtolower(pathinfo($path, PATHINFO_EXTENSION));
    switch ($ext) {
        case 'jpg':
        case 'jpeg':
            imagejpeg($dst, $path, 90);
            break;
        case 'png':
            imagepng($dst, $path, 6);
            break;
        case 'gif':
            imagegif($dst, $path);
            break;
        case 'webp':
            imagewebp($dst, $path, 90);
            break;
    }
    
    imagedestroy($src);
    imagedestroy($dst);
    
    return true;
}

--
-- Structure de la table `ami`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `ami`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `ami` (
  `id` int NOT NULL,
  `idami` int NOT NULL,
  `demandeami` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `accepterami` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `date_demande` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `date_acceptation` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`,`idami`),
  KEY `idx_ami` (`idami`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `communautes`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `communautes`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `communautes` (
  `id_communaute` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `nom` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `description` text,
  `image_couverture` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `categorie` enum('Academic','Club','Social','Sports') DEFAULT 'Academic',
  `id_createur` int NOT NULL,
  `date_creation` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_communaute`),
  KEY `idx_categorie` (`categorie`),
  KEY `id_createur` (`id_createur`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `communaute_membres`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `communaute_membres`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `communaute_membres` (
  `id_communaute` int NOT NULL,
  `id_utilisateur` int NOT NULL,
  `date_joint` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_communaute`,`id_utilisateur`),
  KEY `id_utilisateur` (`id_utilisateur`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `message`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `message`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `message` (
  `idmessage` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `id_expediteur` int NOT NULL,
  `id_destinataire` int NOT NULL,
  `textemessage` text,
  `id_ressource` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `lu` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `datemessage` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `type` varchar(20) DEFAULT 'text',
  `file_url` varchar(500) DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_type` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_size` bigint DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_duration` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_for_sender` tinyint DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted_for_receiver` tinyint DEFAULT '0',
  `file_metadata` text,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idmessage`),
  KEY `idx_expediteur` (`id_expediteur`),
  KEY `idx_destinataire` (`id_destinataire`),
  KEY `idx_lu` (`lu`),
  KEY `id_ressource` (`id_ressource`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=7 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

-- Structure de la table `notifications`

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `notifications`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `notifications` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int NOT NULL,
  `actor_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `type` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `item_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `content` text,
  `is_read` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `password_resets`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `password_resets`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `password_resets` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `expires_at` datetime NOT NULL,
  `used` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `unique_token` (`token`),
  KEY `idx_user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `idx_token` (`token`),
  KEY `idx_expires_at` (`expires_at`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `postcommentaire`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `postcommentaire`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `postcommentaire` (
  `idcommentaire` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `idpost` int NOT NULL,
  `id` int NOT NULL,
  `textecommentaire` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `datecommentaire` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idcommentaire`),
  KEY `idx_post` (`idpost`),
  KEY `id` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `postlike`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `postlike`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `postlike` (
  `idlike` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `idpost` int NOT NULL,
  `id` int NOT NULL,
  `datelike` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`idlike`),
  UNIQUE KEY `unique_like` (`idpost`,`id`),
  KEY `id` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

-- Structure de la table `posts`

  `contenu` text NOT NULL,
  `image_post` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_publication` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

  KEY `idx_utilisateur` (`id_utilisateur`),
  KEY `idx_date` (`date_publication`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

  PRIMARY KEY (`id_ressource`),
  KEY `idx_proprietaire` (`id_proprietaire`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

--
-- Structure de la table `utilisateurs`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `utilisateurs`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `utilisateurs` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `avatar` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT 'default-avatar.png',
  `surnom` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `motdepasse` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `prenom` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `nom` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `profession` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT 'Etudiant',
  `universite` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `faculte` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `niveau_etude` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `role` enum('etudiant','professeur','admin') CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT 'etudiant',
  `nationalite` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `telephone` varchar(15) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `datedenaissance` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `sexe` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `bio` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci,
  `dateinscription` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `status` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT 'Offline',
  `remember_token` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `remember_token_expires` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `dateconnexion` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_ip` varchar(45) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `failed_login_attempts` int DEFAULT '0',
  `locked_until` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_verified` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `is_active` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '1',
  `two_factor_secret` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`),
  KEY `idx_email` (`email`),
  KEY `idx_role` (`role`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2975 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--
-- Contraintes pour les tables déchargées
--

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `activity_logs`
--
ALTER TABLE `activity_logs`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `activity_logs_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `utilisateurs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE;

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `ami`
--
ALTER TABLE `ami`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `ami_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`id`) REFERENCES `utilisateurs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `ami_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`idami`) REFERENCES `utilisateurs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE;

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `communautes`
--
ALTER TABLE `communautes`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `communautes_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`id_createur`) REFERENCES `utilisateurs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE;

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `communaute_membres`
--
ALTER TABLE `communaute_membres`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `communaute_membres_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`id_communaute`) REFERENCES `communautes` (`id_communaute`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `communaute_membres_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`id_utilisateur`) REFERENCES `utilisateurs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE;

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `message`
--
ALTER TABLE `message`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `message_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`id_expediteur`) REFERENCES `utilisateurs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `message_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`id_destinataire`) REFERENCES `utilisateurs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  ADD CONSTRAINT `message_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`id_ressource`) REFERENCES `ressources` (`id_ressource`) ON DELETE SET NULL;

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `notifications`
--
